# LA Alliance Invoices  Before / After

Left: an unstructured scanned invoice the county published as a PDF.
Right: the normalized ledger row our agent extracted autonomously.

##  Social Model Recovery Systems Inc. - Recovery Bridge Housing - December 2024

**Source:** `https://file.lacounty.gov/SDSInter/ceo/asp/1179595_SocialModelRecoverySystemsInc.-RecoveryBridgeHousing-December2024.pdf`  ñ  293.8 KB scanned PDF

| Field | Extracted value |
|-------|-----------------|
| Vendor | SOCIAL MODEL RECOVERY SYSTEMS, INC. |
| Invoice date | 2024-12-31 |
| Billed amount | $109949.50 |
| Deliverables | Recovery Bridge Housing (H2034) |
| Confidence | high |
| Notes | This document is a data export or billing ledger for services rendered, not a single traditional invoice. The 'vendor' is consistently listed as 'SOCIAL MODEL RECOVERY SYSTEMS, INC.'. The 'invoice_date' is derived from the header 'December 2024' and the 'Date of Service' column which spans 2024-12-01 to 2024-12-31. The latest date, 2024-12-31, is used to represent the period covered. The 'billed_amount' is calculated by summing all 'Total Charge' line items (1819 entries * $60.50 each). The 'deliverables' are consistently stated as 'Recovery Bridge Housing (H2034)' across all line items. |
